<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sources">Sources</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Climate_change_adaptation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Sources">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relevant_IPCC_reports">Relevant IPCC reports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Climate_change_adaptation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Relevant IPCC reports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Intergovernmental_Panel_on_Climate_Change" title="Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change">Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change (IPCC)</a> produced two separate reports: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.grida.no/climate/ipcc_tar/wg3/004.htm">Climate Change 2001: Mitigation</a> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.grida.no/climate/ipcc_tar/wg2/006.htm">Climate Change 2001: Impacts, Adaptation and Vulnerability</a></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relevant_United_States_sources">Relevant United States sources</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Climate_change_adaptation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Relevant United States sources">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.usgcrp.gov/usgcrp/default.php">US Global Change Research Program</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.usgcrp.gov/usgcrp/Library/nationalassessment/foundation.htm">US National Assessment—Preparing for a Changing Climate report</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ncgia.ucsb.edu/pubs/CA_Report.pdf">California Regional Assessment: Preparing for Climate Change: The Potential Consequences of Climate Variability and Change for California</a> (not on Federal site) 2002</li>
<li>The US <a href="/wiki/Office_of_Technology_Assessment" title="Office of Technology Assessment">Office of Technology Assessment</a> (OTA) published two reports containing detailed assessments of mitigation and adaptation strategies
<ul>
<li>"Changing by Degrees" investigates options for controlling emissions of carbon dioxide, the most troublesome anthropogenic greenhouse gas (OTA 1991).</li>
<li>"Preparing for an Uncertain Climate" examines how managed natural resource systems—such as water, agriculture, and forests—might adapt to changing environmental conditions brought about by global warming (OTA 1993).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.GeorgetownClimate.org/Adaptation/clearinghouse">Adaptation Clearinghouse of the Georgetown Climate Center</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wildlifeadaptationstrategy.gov/pdf/NFWPCAS-Final.pdf">"National Fish, Wildlife and Plants Climate Adaptation Strategy" 2012</a>
<ul>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wildlifeadaptationstrategy.gov/pdf/Strategy-Highlights-Brochure.pdf">Summary brochure</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_government_sources">Other government sources</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Climate_change_adaptation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Other government sources">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Several countries have taken a lead in climate vulnerability assessment and adaptation planning. Their web sites contain reports, strategies, and tools which other countries can customize to their own situation.</p>
<ul>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ukcip.org.uk/">The United Kingdom's Climate Impacts Programme</a> (UKCIP)</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.greenhouse.gov.au/impacts/">Australia</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.adaptation.nrcan.gc.ca/index_e.php">Canada</a></li>
<li>The Canadian National Assessment: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.adaptation.nrcan.gc.ca/assess/2007/index_e.php">From Impacts to Adaptation: Canada in a Changing Climate 2007</a> discusses current and future risks and opportunities that climate change presents to Canada, with a focus on human and managed systems.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_relevant_sources">Other relevant sources</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Climate_change_adaptation&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Other relevant sources">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In addition to government and United Nations reports, an extensive research literature assesses options for response to global warming. Much of this literature addresses the potential economic costs associated with different strategies.</p>
<ul>
<li>The World Bank has worked with developing countries to support adaptation planning since 1999. It has also analyzed how to mainstream adaptation planning into its loan and grant programs. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://web.worldbank.org/WBSITE/EXTERNAL/TOPICS/ENVIRONMENT/EXTCC/0,,contentMDK:20484574%7EmenuPK:1172760%7EpagePK:148956%7EpiPK:216618%7EtheSitePK:407864,00.html">This page has publications to download</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a> is also working on a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldbank.org/eca/climateandagriculture">Regional Program to Reduce the Vulnerability of Agricultural Systems to Climate Change in the Europe and Central Asia Region</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Asian_Development_Bank" title="Asian Development Bank">Asian Development Bank</a> has a series of studies on the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.adb.org/publications/economics-climate-change-east-asia">Economics of Climate Change</a> in the Asia-Pacific region. The studies provide cost analysis of both adaptation and mitigation measures.</li>
<li>Indigo Development has a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.indigodev.com/climadaptlinks.html">page of links to government and research web sites on climate adaptation</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Oxfam" title="Oxfam">Oxfam</a> has issued a report detailing the need for high emissions countries to support adaptation in developing countries: Adapting to climate change, What's needed in poor countries, and who should pay Oxfam Briefing Paper 104</li>
<li>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.eldis.org/go/topics">Eldis platform</a>, run by the Institute of Development Studies at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Sussex" title="University of Sussex">University of Sussex</a> has literature on adaptation and sustainable development</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/WEAP" title="WEAP">WEAP</a> (Water Evaluation And Planning system) assists water resources researchers and planners in assessing impacts of and adaptations to climate change.</li>
<li>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.weadapt.org/">weADAPT platform</a> encourages the collaborative development of tools for adaptation and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wikiadapt.org/">sharing experiences from adaptation projects</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/UNDP" class="mw-redirect" title="UNDP">UNDP</a> runs the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.adaptationlearning.net/">adaptation learning mechanism</a> which provides country case studies of adaptation.</li>
<li>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://cecar.unu.edu/">UN-CECAR</a> research and development of courses on climate change and adaptation</li>
<li>The UNFCCC has a database on <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://maindb.unfccc.int/public/adaptation/">local adaptation measures</a> and information on <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://unfccc.int/adaptation/items/4159.phpadaptation">the international climate negotiations</a></li>
<li>"Economic Approaches to Greenhouse Warming" provides a summary of Yale economist <a href="/wiki/William_Nordhaus" title="William Nordhaus">William Nordhaus</a>' ideas (1991). Nordhaus questions the motivation for countries to pursue relatively costly measures for responding to global warming given current scientific uncertainty about the problem's magnitude and estimates potential economic impacts may not be that high, particularly for <a href="/wiki/Developed_economies" class="mw-redirect" title="Developed economies">developed economies</a>.</li>
<li>Economist <a href="/wiki/William_R._Cline" title="William R. Cline">William R. Cline</a> offers an opposing view, arguing potential economic costs of unabated global warming could be very high. In the monograph, "Global Warming: The Economic Stakes", Cline (1992) assesses the potential cost of damages from global warming and the cost of efforts to control greenhouse gas emissions.</li>
<li>"Coping with Global Climate Change: The Role of Adaptation in the United States" <a href="/wiki/Pew_Center_on_Global_Climate_Change" class="mw-redirect" title="Pew Center on Global Climate Change">Pew Center on Global Climate Change</a>, June 2004.</li>
<li>National Center for Policy Analysis <cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ncpa.org/pub/st/st278/">"Living with Global Warming"</a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AClimate+change+adaptation&amp;rft.btitle=Living+with+Global+Warming&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.ncpa.org%2Fpub%2Fst%2Fst278%2F&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook" class="Z3988"><span style="display:none;">&#160;</span></span></li>
<li>"Adaptation to Global Warming" James Titus<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Words_to_watch#Unsupported_attributions" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Words to watch"><span title="The material near this tag possibly uses too-vague attribution or weasel words. (August 2011)">who?</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>"Climate's Long-Lost Twin" Richard Monastersky<sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Words_to_watch#Unsupported_attributions" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Words to watch"><span title="The material near this tag possibly uses too-vague attribution or weasel words. (September 2011)">who?</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
<li>Heintz Foundation, 2007 <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.heinzctr.org/publications/PDF/Adaptation_Report_October_10_2007.pdf">A Survey of Climate Change Adaptation Planning</a> pdf</li>
<li>"Adapt or Die: The Science, Politics and Economics of Climate Change" Profile Books, December 2003 <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/1861977956" class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn">ISBN 1-86197-795-6</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/USDA" class="mw-redirect" title="USDA">USDA</a> Economic Research Service <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ers.usda.gov/publications/tb1909/">Economics of Sequestering Carbon in the U.S. Agricultural Sector</a></li>
<li>USDA Economic Research Service <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ers.usda.gov/publications/aer740/">Agricultural Adaptation to Climate Change: Issues of Longrun Sustainability</a></li>
<li>USDA Economic Research Service <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ers.usda.gov/publications/aer703/">World Agriculture and Climate Change: Economic Adaptations</a></li>
<li>"Policy Implications of Greenhouse Warming." <a href="/wiki/United_States_National_Academy_of_Sciences" class="mw-redirect" title="United States National Academy of Sciences">United States National Academy of Sciences</a>, 1991.</li>
<li>"Water Allocation in a Changing Climate: Institutions and Adaptation" <a href="/wiki/Springer_Netherlands" class="mw-redirect" title="Springer Netherlands">Springer Netherlands</a>, ISSN 0165-0009 (Paper) 1573-1480 (Online) Volume 35, Number 2, February 1997. pp.&#160;157&#160;– 177.</li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.epa.gov/eims/global/clim_res.pdf">Risks, opportunities, and adaptation to climate change</a> Joel D. Scheraga, Anne E. Grambsch, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Environmental_Protection_Agency" title="United States Environmental Protection Agency">United States Environmental Protection Agency</a>.</li>
<li>McMichael <i>et al.</i> (2003). <i>Climate Change and Human Health&#160;– Risk and Responses</i>. <a href="/wiki/WHO" class="mw-redirect" title="WHO">WHO</a>, <a href="/wiki/UNEP" class="mw-redirect" title="UNEP">UNEP</a>, <a href="/wiki/WMO" class="mw-redirect" title="WMO">WMO</a>, Geneva. <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9241590815" class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn">ISBN 92-4-159081-5</a>.</li>
<li>Müller, B. (2002) <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.oxfordclimatepolicy.org/publications/documents/The_Great_Divide-Executive_Summary.pdf">Equity in Climate Change. The Great Divide</a>. <a href="/wiki/Oxford_Institute_for_Energy_Studies" title="Oxford Institute for Energy Studies">Oxford Institute for Energy Studies</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.oxfordenergy.org/">[2]</a>. Oxford, UK</li>
<li>House of Lords Select Committee on Economic Affairs, 2nd Report of Session 2005-6 <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.publications.parliament.uk/pa/ld200506/ldselect/ldeconaf/12/12i.pdf">The Economics of Climate Change. Volume I: Report</a> pdf</li>
<li>Rivington M, Matthews KB, Buchan K and Miller D (2005) <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.macaulay.ac.uk/LADSS/papers.html?2005">"An integrated assessment approach to investigate options for mitigation and adaptation to climate change at the farm-scale"</a>, NJF Seminar 380, <a href="/wiki/Odense" title="Odense">Odense</a>, Denmark, 7–8 November 2005, via <a href="/wiki/Macaulay_Institute" title="Macaulay Institute">Macaulay Institute</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Land_Allocation_Decision_Support_System" title="Land Allocation Decision Support System">Land Allocation Decision Support System</a>.</li>
<li>Ludwig, Fulco, Pavel Kabat, Henk van Schaik and Michael van der Valk (2009) <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.hydrology.nl/ihppublications/125-climate-change-adaptation-in-the-water-sector.html">Climate Change Adaptation in the Water Sector</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.earthscan.co.uk/?tabid=34059">Earthscan</a>, London, 320 pp, <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781844076529" class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn">ISBN 978-1-84407-652-9</a>.</li>
<li>Amy Seidl <i>Finding Higher Ground: Adaptation in the Age of Warming</i> <a href="/wiki/Beacon_Press" title="Beacon Press">Beacon Press</a> (June 7, 2011) <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9780807085981" class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn">ISBN 978-0-8070-8598-1</a></li>
<li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.hydrology.nl/cpwcpublications.html">Publications by the Co-operative Programme on Water and Climate (CPWC)</a></li>
</ul>
